[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocesses certificate data in PEM format. Specifically:[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Evaluation Report and Code Snippets[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability and the provided code [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msnippets, I've identified the root causes and the optimal fix strategy.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Causes Identified[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Buffer Overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m452[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m457[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m452[0m[39m allocates memory based on `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which stops at the first null [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m457[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[39m copy data based on `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which returns the full[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mASN1 string length including embedded nulls[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When ASN1 strings contain embedded null bytes, `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns a smaller [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue than `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, causing heap-buffer-overflow[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Missing Null Termination**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After `memcpy`, the buffer is not null-terminated[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `verify_san` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m893[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which requires [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull-terminated strings[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This causes reading beyond allocated buffer bounds[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Incorrect Return Value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m473[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Function always returns `TRUE` regardless of validation result[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m correctly sets `result = FALSE` on validation failure[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m473[0m[39m ignores `result` variable by returning `TRUE` unconditionally[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This undermines the security check, allowing malformed certificates to be [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccepted[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Code Duplication and Pattern Inconsistency**:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function manually implements DNS name extraction using unsafe methods[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The codebase already has correct implementations: `extract_string` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m280[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m320[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `x509_utils_get_dns_names` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m561[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m598[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These use `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` API correctly with proper memory management[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security validation**: The function serves as a security gate - must reject [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcertificates with invalid DNS names[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error propagation**: When called from `freerdp_rsa_from_x509` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1259[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailure must propagate to prevent certificate acceptance[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **SAN iteration**: Must validate ALL DNS names in Subject Alternative Names[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Cleanup**: Must properly free OpenSSL structures with [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`sk_GENERAL_NAME_pop_free`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why Previous Patches Don't Apply[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis appears to be the initial report, so no previous patches exist. However, the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode analysis reveals that the vulnerability exists because the implementation [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoesn't follow the established patterns in the codebase for ASN1 string handling.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI will implement **Approach [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Refactor to Use Existing Functions** as this is the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moptimal solution.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Replace manual DNS extraction with `x509_utils_get_dns_names`**[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove lines [0m[1;36m436[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m440[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m468[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmanual iteration and unsafe string handling[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call `[0m[1;35mx509_utils_get_dns_names[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert, &count, &lengths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to get all DNS names[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This function uses the correct `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` pattern internally[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Iterate and validate DNS names**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop through the returned DNS names array[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call `[0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on each DNS name[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Set `result = FALSE` and break on first validation failure[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All strings are properly null-terminated by `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Proper cleanup**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call `[0m[1;35mx509_utils_dns_names_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcount, lengths, dns_names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to free resources[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This correctly uses `[0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for OpenSSL-allocated strings[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Return the `result` variable [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot hardcoded `TRUE`[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Handle edge cases**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `x509_utils_get_dns_names` returns NULL [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno DNS names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, return TRUE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalid [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If allocation fails within `x509_utils_get_dns_names`, return TRUE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfail-safe: no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation is better than false negatives for this security check[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Detailed Fix for libfreerdp/crypto/x509_utils.[0m[1;92mc:433[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m474[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBOOL [0m[1;35mx509_validate_subject_aternative_names[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst X509* cert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    BOOL result = TRUE;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    size_t count = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    size_t* lengths = NULL;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Use existing function to extract DNS names correctly[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    char** dns_names = [0m[1;35mx509_utils_get_dns_names[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert, &count, &lengths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m No DNS names is a valid case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcertificate may not have SAN extension[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!dns_names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return TRUE;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate each DNS name[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < count; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_names[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            result = FALSE;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            break;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Stop on first invalid DNS name[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Proper cleanup with correct free functions[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mx509_utils_dns_names_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcount, lengths, dns_names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return result;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is The Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates All Root Causes**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer overflow: `x509_utils_get_dns_names` uses `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternally [0m[1;39m([0m[39msafe API[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Null termination: `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` returns properly null-terminated UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Return value: Returns `result` variable, not hardcoded `TRUE`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Code duplication: Reuses existing, tested functions[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Established Codebase Patterns**:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same pattern used in `x509_utils_get_common_name` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m850[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m868[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consistent with how the codebase handles ASN1 string conversion[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses existing helper functions designed for this purpose[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes, Maximum Safety**:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reduces code from ~[0m[1;36m41[0m[39m lines to ~[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m lines[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates unsafe manual memory management[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leverages battle-tested utility functions[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external dependencies or API changes needed[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still validates all DNS names in SANs[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still calls `[0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for validation[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still returns FALSE on validation failure[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still allows certificates without DNS names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturns TRUE[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Memory Management Correctness**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `x509_utils_get_dns_names` allocates with `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOpenSSL [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `x509_utils_dns_names_free` correctly uses `[0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for each string[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No memory leaks, no use-after-free, no double-free[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses Issues in Evaluation Report[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Heap-buffer-overflow**: Eliminated by using `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` which [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocates correct size[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m-byte write to [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m-byte buffer**: Won't occur because allocation size matches [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata size[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m452[0m[39m allocation issue**: Removed - using correct API[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m457[0m[39m memcpy overflow**: Removed - no manual memcpy[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m473[0m[39m return value bug**: Fixed - returns `result` variable[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Performance**: Slightly more overhead from creating intermediate arrays[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Negligible impact - certificate parsing is not [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance-critical[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only occurs during certificate validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39minfrequent operation[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **API compatibility**: Changes internal implementation only[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Function signature unchanged, callers unaffected[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still declared in x509_utils.h:[0m[1;36m61[0m[39m, no header changes needed[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Error handling**: Now returns TRUE if DNS extraction fails[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Fail-safe approach - better to allow connection than false [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreject[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consistent with line [0m[1;36m442[0m[39m behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturns TRUE if no SAN extension[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Validation semantics**: Breaks on first invalid DNS name [0m[1;39m([0m[39mshort-circuit [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevaluation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Correct behavior - one invalid DNS name invalidates entire [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcertificate[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consistent with security best practices[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis pattern is used in multiple places:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m850[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m868[0m[39m**: `x509_utils_get_common_name` uses `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` + [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`_strdup` + `OPENSSL_free`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m561[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m598[0m[39m**: `x509_utils_get_dns_names` uses `map_subject_alt_name` + [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`extract_string`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m280[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m320[0m[39m**: `extract_string` uses `ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8` + error handling[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix applies the same proven pattern to the vulnerable function.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
